&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Mandate Processing Outcomes&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Mandate Resolution Notifications&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;MPIR Processing Outcomes&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;PayTo Query Notifications&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Payloads will be encrypted and signed prior to transmitting. Customers will need to decrypt the payload and verify the signature prior to processing the Processing Outcome or Notification.&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Processing Outcomes and Notifications may arrive out of sequence and may be delivered more than once. ANZ will attempt to deliver each Processing Outcome and Notification at least once.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>Fileactive PayTo API Webhook provides consumers the ability to receive:<br></p>
<ul>
<li>Mandate Processing Outcomes</li>
<li>Mandate Resolution Notifications</li>
<li>MPIR Processing Outcomes</li>
<li>PayTo Query Notifications<br><br></li>
</ul>
<p>Payloads will be encrypted and signed prior to transmitting. Customers will need to decrypt the payload and verify the signature prior to processing the Processing Outcome or Notification.<br></p>
<p>Processing Outcomes and Notifications may arrive out of sequence and may be delivered more than once. ANZ will attempt to deliver each Processing Outcome and Notification at least once.</p>

"><p>Operations related to mandates.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/Mandate/operation/mandateOutcomes" data-section-id="tag/Mandate/operation/mandateOutcomes" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/mandateOutcomes" id="operation/mandateOutcomes" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate/operation/mandateOutcomes" aria-label="tag/Mandate/operation/mandateOutcomes"></a>Mandate Processing Outcomes.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to provide the processing outcome of the following mandate actions initiated by the &lt;strong&gt;Payee&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Create Mandate&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Change Mandate Status&lt;br&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Duplicate checking should be based on the &lt;code&gt;request_id&lt;/code&gt;, i.e. the &lt;strong&gt;Payee&lt;/strong&gt; identifiyer provided in the original mandate request.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to provide the processing outcome of the following mandate actions initiated by the <strong>Payee</strong>:<br></p>
<ul>
<li>Create Mandate</li>
<li>Change Mandate Status<br></li>
</ul>
<p>Duplicate checking should be based on the <code>request_id</code>, i.e. the <strong>Payee</strong> identifiyer provided in the original mandate request.</p>

data-section-id="tag/Mandate/operation/mandateNotifications" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/mandateNotifications" id="operation/mandateNotifications" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate/operation/mandateNotifications" aria-label="tag/Mandate/operation/mandateNotifications"></a>Mandate Notifications.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to provide a notification where the &lt;strong&gt;Payer&lt;/strong&gt; has taken an action on a Mandate. The following notifications are supported:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Bilateral Create Mandate Resolution&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Bilateral Create Mandate Timeout&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Unilateral Amend Mandate &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Unilateral Change Mandate Status&lt;br&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Duplicate checking should be based on &lt;strong&gt;MMS&lt;/strong&gt; assigined identfier &lt;code&gt;action_identification&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to provide a notification where the <strong>Payer</strong> has taken an action on a Mandate. The following notifications are supported:</p>
<ul>
<li>Bilateral Create Mandate Resolution</li>
<li>Bilateral Create Mandate Timeout</li>
<li>Unilateral Amend Mandate </li>
<li>Unilateral Change Mandate Status<br></li>
</ul>
<p>Duplicate checking should be based on <strong>MMS</strong> assigined identfier <code>action_identification</code></p>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG"><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Message-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Message-Id</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">3d003c66-2d00-4092-8d8a-e55ba9bf8b2b</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="priority" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">priority</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->NotificationPriority1Code<!-- -->) </span></div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;ATTENDED&quot;</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;UNATTENDED&quot;</span> </div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. This value does not affect the priority for processing within the MMS. It may, depending on topic configuration, influence which topic any generated notification is sent to.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. This value does not affect the priority for processing within the MMS. role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-19" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-18"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/MPIR" data-section-id="tag/MPIR" class="sc-eDLKkx hNzKJC"><div class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/MPIR" aria-label="tag/MPIR"></a>MPIR</h1></div></div></div><div id="tag/MPIR/operation/mandateOutcomes" data-section-id="tag/MPIR/operation/mandateOutcomes" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/mandateOutcomes" id="operation/mandateOutcomes" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/MPIR/operation/mandateOutcomes" aria-label="tag/MPIR/operation/mandateOutcomes"></a>MPIR Processing Outcomes.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to provide the processing outcome of the following MPIR actions initiated by the &lt;strong&gt;Payee&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Create MPIR&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If MPIR is processed same day and successfully settles then &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; will be &lt;strong&gt;ACSC&lt;/strong&gt; Settlement Completed.&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If MPIR is future dated then &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; will be &lt;strong&gt;PDNG&lt;/strong&gt; Warehoused. This will be followed by the settlement processing outcome once &lt;code&gt;requested_execution_date&lt;/code&gt; is reached.&lt;br&gt; &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If MPIR settlement is delayed then &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; will be &lt;strong&gt;ACSP&lt;/strong&gt; Settlement Pending. This will be followed by the settlement processing outcome.&lt;br&gt; &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If MPIR is invalid or fails settlement then &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; will be &lt;strong&gt;RJCT&lt;/strong&gt; Rejected. The &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; will incidcate the reason for rejection.&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Duplicate checking should be based on &lt;strong&gt;Payee&lt;/strong&gt; assigined identfier &lt;code&gt;instruction_identification&lt;/code&gt;/ &lt;code&gt;uetr&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;transaction_status_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; &lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Payee should also consider Processing Outcomes for the same MPIR arrving out of sequence.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to provide the processing outcome of the following MPIR actions initiated by the <strong>Payee</strong>:<br></p>
<ul>
<li>Create MPIR</li>
</ul>
<p>If MPIR is processed same day and successfully settles then <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> will be <strong>ACSC</strong> Settlement Completed.<br></p>
<p>If MPIR is future dated then <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> will be <strong>PDNG</strong> Warehoused. This will be followed by the settlement processing outcome once <code>requested_execution_date</code> is reached.<br> </p>
<p>If MPIR settlement is delayed then <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> will be <strong>ACSP</strong> Settlement Pending. This will be followed by the settlement processing outcome.<br> </p>
<p>If MPIR is invalid or fails settlement then <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> will be <strong>RJCT</strong> Rejected. The <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> will incidcate the reason for rejection.<br><br></p>
<p>Duplicate checking should be based on <strong>Payee</strong> assigined identfier <code>instruction_identification</code>/ <code>uetr</code> and <code>transaction_status_reason_code</code> <br><br></p>
<p>Payee should also consider Processing Outcomes for the same MPIR arrving out of sequence.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG"><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-RequestKey" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-RequestKey</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">325ea624-ac19-47e2-94ef-a1ab4e487275</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Internal End to End key used for support and reporting purposes.             &lt;/p&gt;

fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Query" aria-label="tag/Query"></a>Query</h1></div></div></div><div id="tag/Query/operation/mandateQueries" data-section-id="tag/Query/operation/mandateQueries" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/mandateQueries" id="operation/mandateQueries" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Query/operation/mandateQueries" aria-label="tag/Query/operation/mandateQueries"></a>PayTo Queries.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to provide a notification where the &lt;strong&gt;Payer&lt;/strong&gt; has raised a PayTo query via the &lt;strong&gt;Payer&amp;#39;s&lt;/strong&gt; Financial Institution. The following notifications are supported:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Mandate Query&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Mandate Query Payment&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Duplicate checking should be based on &lt;strong&gt;ANZ&lt;/strong&gt; assigined identfier &lt;code&gt;case_id&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;reminder_count&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;re_open_case_indication&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to provide a notification where the <strong>Payer</strong> has raised a PayTo query via the <strong>Payer&#39;s</strong> Financial Institution. The following notifications are supported:</p>
<ul>
<li>Mandate Query</li>
<li>Mandate Query Payment</li>
</ul>
<p>Duplicate checking should be based on <strong>ANZ</strong> assigined identfier <code>case_id</code> and <code>reminder_count</code> and <code>re_open_case_indication</code></p>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG"><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Message-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Message-Id</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">3d003c66-2d00-4092-8d8a-e55ba9bf8b2b</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message&lt;/p&gt;

Urgency or order of importance that the originator would like the recipient of the PayTo query to apply to the processing of the query.&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt; Only &lt;strong&gt;UNATTENDED&lt;/strong&gt; is supported for this notification type.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. &lt;li&gt;A port that has been finalised.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;DECL&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Declined&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Action has been declined.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;PEND&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Pending&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;This status represents the following situations:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;A bilateral action that is waiting to be confirmed.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;A porting action that has been initiated and is waiting to be finalised.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;RECL&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Recalled&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Action has been recalled.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;TIMO&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;TimedOut&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Action was created bilaterally and has now timed out.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Enumeration of the states that a mandate action can have.</p>
<table><tr><th>Code</th><th>Name</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td>CMPL</td><td>Completed</td><td><p>This status represents the following situations:</p>
<ul>
<li>A bilateral action that has been confirmed.</li>
<li>A unilateral action has been performed.</li>
<li>A port that has been finalised.</li>
</ul>
</td></tr><tr><td>DECL</td><td>Declined</td><td>Action has been declined.</td></tr><tr><td>PEND</td><td>Pending</td><td><p>This status represents the following situations:</p>
<ul>
<li>A bilateral action that is waiting to be confirmed.</li>
<li>A porting action that has been initiated and is waiting to be finalised.</li>
</ul>
</td></tr><tr><td>RECL</td><td>Recalled</td><td>Action has been recalled.</td></tr><tr><td>TIMO</td><td>TimedOut</td><td>Action was created bilaterally and has now timed out.</td></tr></table></div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="bilateral" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">bilateral</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">boolean</span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Boolean flag indicating if the action was created as bilateral or unilateral. Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID) version 1, as described in IETC RFC 4122 &amp;quot;Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID) URN Namespace&amp;quot; without the 4 hyphen separators.
For example: &amp;#39;00000000000010008000000000000000&amp;#39; instead of  &amp;#39;00000000-0000-1000-8000-000000000000&amp;#39; (without quotes)&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Unique ID assigned to the mandate request action. This ID is used to uniquely identify the action for all further operations on a mandate action.
Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID) version 1, as described in IETC RFC 4122 &quot;Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID) URN Namespace&quot; without the 4 hyphen separators.
For example: &#39;00000000000010008000000000000000&#39; instead of  &#39;00000000-0000-1000-8000-000000000000&#39; (without quotes)</p>
